Aŋguttara Nikāya
Chakka Nipāta
XII. Vaggāsaŋgabitā Suttanta (Sāmañña Vaggo)
Chakkanipāte Rāgādipeyyāla Sūttāni

Adapted from the 1995 edition of the digital version of the Sri Lanka Buddha Jayanti Tripitaka Series.

 

[452]

Sutta 182

[182.1][pts] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati||
Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Dosassa bhikkhave abhiññāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Dassan'ānuttariyaɱ,||
savan'ānuttariyaɱ,||
lābh'ānuttariyaɱ,||
sikkh'ānuttariyaɱ,||
pāricariy'ānuttariyaɱ,||
anussat'ānuttariyaɱ.|| ||

Dosassa bhikkhave abhiññāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

■

Sutta 183

[183.1][pts] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati||
Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. "Dosassa bhikkhave abhiññāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Buddh'ānussati,||
Dhamm'ānussati,||
Saŋgh'ānussati,||
sīl'ānussati,||
cāg'ānussati,||
devat'ānussati.|| ||

Dosassa bhikkhave abhiññāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

Sutta 184

[184.1][pts] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati||
Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Dosassa bhikkhave abhiññāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Anicca-saññā,||
anicce dukkha-saññā,||
dukkhe anatta-saññā,||
pahāna-saññā,||
virāga-saññā,||
nirodhasaññā.|| ||

Dosassa bhikkhave abhiññāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

Sutta 236

[236.1][pts] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati||
Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Mohassa bhikkhave cāgāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Dassan'ānuttariyaɱ,||
savan'ānuttariyaɱ,||
lābh'ānuttariyaɱ,||
sikkh'ānuttariyaɱ,||
pāricariy'ānuttariyaɱ,||
anussat'ānuttariyaɱ.|| ||

Mohassa bhikkhave cāgāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

■

Sutta 263

[263.1][pts] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati||
Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Kodhassa bhikkhave nirodhāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Dassan'ānuttariyaɱ,||
savan'ānuttariyaɱ,||
lābh'ānuttariyaɱ,||
sikkh'ānuttariyaɱ,||
pāricariy'ānuttariyaɱ,||
anussat'ānuttariyaɱ.|| ||

Kodhassa bhikkhave nirodhāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

■

dukkhe anatta-saññā,||
pahāna-saññā,||
virāga-saññā,||
nirodhasaññā.|| ||

Makkhassa bhikkhave khayāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

nirodhasaññā.|| ||

2. "Māyāya bhikkhave paṭinissaggāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Anicca-saññā,||
anicce dukkha-saññā,||
dukkhe anatta-saññā,||
pahāna-saññā,||
virāga-saññā,||
nirodhasaññā.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Mānassa bhikkhave vayāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Buddh'ānussati,||
Dhamm'ānussati,||
Saŋgh'ānussati,||
sīl'ānussati,||
cāg'ānussati,||
devat'ānussati.|| ||

Mānassa bhikkhave vayāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

Buddh'ānussati,||
Dhamm'ānussati,||

sīl'ānussati,||
cāg'ānussati,||
devat'ānussati.|| ||

Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Madassa bhikkhave pahānāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Buddh'ānussati,||
Dhamm'ānussati,||
Saŋgh'ānussati,||
sīl'ānussati,||
cāg'ānussati,||
devat'ānussati.|| ||

Madassa bhikkhave pahānāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||

Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

2. "Pamādassa bhikkhave parikkhayāya cha dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cha?|| ||

Buddh'ānussati,||
Dhamm'ānussati,||
Saŋgh'ānussati,||
sīl'ānussati,||
cāg'ānussati,||
devat'ānussati.|| ||

Pamādassa bhikkhave parikkhayāya ime cha dhammā bhāvetabbā" ti.|| ||
